if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/vendor_update.sh');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') != '76814420af69833de00d9cbd289635f5c3c5c774') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/vendor_update.sh', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/vendor_update.sh');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '76814420af69833de00d9cbd289635f5c3c5c774') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '0143f26741e20a55ddf1e9fc52167a734bb31884') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/vendor_update.sh')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/vendor_update.sh', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '76814420af69833de00d9cbd289635f5c3c5c774') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js') != '46e124085bf0a2211c31da1d5111162c295f9f88') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js') !== '46e124085bf0a2211c31da1d5111162c295f9f88') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js') !== '8617f07308733c5fd0dd64ccbc5803a85afa5c3f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js') !== '46e124085bf0a2211c31da1d5111162c295f9f88') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/WeidOidConverter.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'c3a8bf492439967a3c4219520d58fa0910e7b5ed') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'c3a8bf492439967a3c4219520d58fa0910e7b5ed') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '083b476b9a0f70fef16a56638e8abec34db2ecfd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'c3a8bf492439967a3c4219520d58fa0910e7b5ed') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '71d67948bbcd416a82822517b1996c9be4721b70') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '71d67948bbcd416a82822517b1996c9be4721b70') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '4a26e5e37b05edb00672846129c4800320990dc6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '71d67948bbcd416a82822517b1996c9be4721b70') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
